  window.builderIoAbTest = function updateCookiesAndStyles(contentId, variants, isHydrationTarget, isAngularSDK) {
  function getAndSetVariantId() {
    function setCookie(name, value, days) {
      let expires = '';
      if (days) {
        const date = new Date();
        date.setTime(date.getTime() + days * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000);
        expires = '; expires=' + date.toUTCString();
      }
      document.cookie = name + '=' + (value || '') + expires + '; path=/' + '; Secure; SameSite=None';
    }
    function getCookie(name) {
      const nameEQ = name + '=';
      const ca = document.cookie.split(';');
      for (let i = 0; i < ca.length; i++) {
        let c = ca[i];
        while (c.charAt(0) === ' ') c = c.substring(1, c.length);
        if (c.indexOf(nameEQ) === 0) return c.substring(nameEQ.length, c.length);
      }
      return null;
    }
    const cookieName = `builder.tests.${contentId}`;
    const variantInCookie = getCookie(cookieName);
    const availableIDs = variants.map(vr => vr.id).concat(contentId);
    if (variantInCookie && availableIDs.includes(variantInCookie)) {
      return variantInCookie;
    }
    let n = 0;
    const random = Math.random();
    for (let i = 0; i < variants.length; i++) {
      const variant = variants[i];
      const testRatio = variant.testRatio;
      n += testRatio;
      if (random < n) {
        setCookie(cookieName, variant.id);
        return variant.id;
      }
    }
    setCookie(cookieName, contentId);
    return contentId;
  }
  const winningVariantId = getAndSetVariantId();
  let styleEl = document.currentScript?.previousElementSibling;
  if (isAngularSDK) {
    styleEl = document.currentScript?.parentElement?.previousElementSibling?.querySelector('style');
  }
  if (isHydrationTarget) {
    styleEl.remove();
    const thisScriptEl = document.currentScript;
    thisScriptEl?.remove();
  } else {
    const newStyleStr = variants.concat({
      id: contentId
    }).filter(variant => variant.id !== winningVariantId).map(value => {
      return `.variant-${value.id} {  display: none; }
        `;
    }).join('');
    styleEl.innerHTML = newStyleStr;
  }
}
  window.builderIoRenderContent = function updateVariantVisibility(variantContentId, defaultContentId, isHydrationTarget) {
  if (!navigator.cookieEnabled) {
    return;
  }
  function getCookie(name) {
    const nameEQ = name + '=';
    const ca = document.cookie.split(';');
    for (let i = 0; i < ca.length; i++) {
      let c = ca[i];
      while (c.charAt(0) === ' ') c = c.substring(1, c.length);
      if (c.indexOf(nameEQ) === 0) return c.substring(nameEQ.length, c.length);
    }
    return null;
  }
  const cookieName = `builder.tests.${defaultContentId}`;
  const winningVariant = getCookie(cookieName);
  const parentDiv = document.currentScript?.parentElement;
  const isDefaultContent = variantContentId === defaultContentId;
  const isWinningVariant = winningVariant === variantContentId;
  if (isWinningVariant && !isDefaultContent) {
    parentDiv?.removeAttribute('hidden');
    parentDiv?.removeAttribute('aria-hidden');
  } else if (!isWinningVariant && isDefaultContent) {
    parentDiv?.setAttribute('hidden', 'true');
    parentDiv?.setAttribute('aria-hidden', 'true');
  }
  if (isHydrationTarget) {
    if (!isWinningVariant) {
      parentDiv?.remove();
    }
    const thisScriptEl = document.currentScript;
    thisScriptEl?.remove();
  }
  return;
}
  </script><script data-id="builderio-init-personalization-variants-fns" nonce="">
  window.filterWithCustomTargeting = function filterWithCustomTargeting(userAttributes, query, startDate, endDate) {
  function isString(val) {
    return typeof val === 'string';
  }
  function isNumber(val) {
    return typeof val === 'number';
  }
  function objectMatchesQuery(userattr, query) {
    const result = (() => {
      const property = query.property;
      const operator = query.operator;
      let testValue = query.value;
      if (query && query.property === 'urlPath' && query.value && typeof query.value === 'string' && query.value !== '/' && query.value.endsWith('/')) {
        testValue = query.value.slice(0, -1);
      }
      if (!(property && operator)) {
        return true;
      }
      if (Array.isArray(testValue)) {
        if (operator === 'isNot') {
          return testValue.every(val => objectMatchesQuery(userattr, {
            property,
            operator,
            value: val
          }));
        }
        return !!testValue.find(val => objectMatchesQuery(userattr, {
          property,
          operator,
          value: val
        }));
      }
      const value = userattr[property];
      if (Array.isArray(value)) {
        return value.includes(testValue);
      }
      switch (operator) {
        case 'is':
          return value === testValue;
        case 'isNot':
          return value !== testValue;
        case 'contains':
          return (isString(value) || Array.isArray(value)) && value.includes(String(testValue));
        case 'startsWith':
          return isString(value) && value.startsWith(String(testValue));
        case 'endsWith':
          return isString(value) && value.endsWith(String(testValue));
        case 'greaterThan':
          return isNumber(value) && isNumber(testValue) && value > testValue;
        case 'lessThan':
          return isNumber(value) && isNumber(testValue) && value < testValue;
        case 'greaterThanOrEqualTo':
          return isNumber(value) && isNumber(testValue) && value >= testValue;
        case 'lessThanOrEqualTo':
          return isNumber(value) && isNumber(testValue) && value <= testValue;
        default:
          return false;
      }
    })();
    return result;
  }
  const item = {
    query,
    startDate,
    endDate
  };
  const now = userAttributes.date && new Date(userAttributes.date) || new Date();
  if (item.startDate && new Date(item.startDate) > now) {
    return false;
  } else if (item.endDate && new Date(item.endDate) < now) {
    return false;
  }
  if (!item.query || !item.query.length) {
    return true;
  }
  return item.query.every(filter => {
    return objectMatchesQuery(userAttributes, filter);
  });
}
  window.builderIoPersonalization = function getPersonalizedVariant(variants, blockId, isHydrationTarget, locale) {
  if (!navigator.cookieEnabled) {
    return;
  }
  function getCookie(name) {
    const nameEQ = name + '=';
    const ca = document.cookie.split(';');
    for (let i = 0; i < ca.length; i++) {
      let c = ca[i];
      while (c.charAt(0) == ' ') c = c.substring(1, c.length);
      if (c.indexOf(nameEQ) == 0) return c.substring(nameEQ.length, c.length);
    }
    return null;
  }
  const attributes = JSON.parse(getCookie('builder.userAttributes') || '{}');
  if (locale) {
    attributes.locale = locale;
  }
  const winningVariantIndex = variants?.findIndex(function (variant) {
    return window.filterWithCustomTargeting(attributes, variant.query, variant.startDate, variant.endDate);
  });
  const parentDiv = document.currentScript?.parentElement;
  const variantId = parentDiv?.getAttribute('data-variant-id');
  const isDefaultVariant = variantId === `${blockId}-default`;
  const isWinningVariant = winningVariantIndex !== -1 && variantId === `${blockId}-${winningVariantIndex}` || winningVariantIndex === -1 && isDefaultVariant;
  if (isWinningVariant && !isDefaultVariant) {
    parentDiv?.removeAttribute('hidden');
    parentDiv?.removeAttribute('aria-hidden');
  } else if (!isWinningVariant && isDefaultVariant) {
    parentDiv?.setAttribute('hidden', 'true');
    parentDiv?.setAttribute('aria-hidden', 'true');
  }
  if (isHydrationTarget) {
    if (!isWinningVariant) {
      const itsStyleEl = parentDiv?.previousElementSibling;
      if (itsStyleEl) {
        itsStyleEl.remove();
      }
      parentDiv?.remove();
    }
    const thisScript = document.currentScript;
    if (thisScript) {
      thisScript.remove();
    }
  }
}
  window.updateVisibilityStylesScript = function updateVisibilityStylesScript(variants, blockId, isHydrationTarget, locale) {
  function getCookie(name) {
    const nameEQ = name + '=';
    const ca = document.cookie.split(';');
    for (let i = 0; i < ca.length; i++) {
      let c = ca[i];
      while (c.charAt(0) == ' ') c = c.substring(1, c.length);
      if (c.indexOf(nameEQ) == 0) return c.substring(nameEQ.length, c.length);
    }
    return null;
  }
  const visibilityStylesEl = document.currentScript?.previousElementSibling;
  if (!visibilityStylesEl) {
    return;
  }
  if (isHydrationTarget) {
    visibilityStylesEl.remove();
    const currentScript = document.currentScript;
    if (currentScript) {
      currentScript.remove();
    }
  } else {
    const attributes = JSON.parse(getCookie('builder.userAttributes') || '{}');
    if (locale) {
      attributes.locale = locale;
    }
    const winningVariantIndex = variants?.findIndex(function (variant) {
      return window.filterWithCustomTargeting(attributes, variant.query, variant.startDate, variant.endDate);
    });
    if (winningVariantIndex !== -1) {
      let newStyleStr = variants?.map((_, index) => {
        if (index === winningVariantIndex) return '';
        return `div[data-variant-id="${blockId}-${index}"] { display: none !important; } `;
      }).join('') || '';
      newStyleStr += `div[data-variant-id="${blockId}-default"] { display: none !important; } `;
      visibilityStylesEl.innerHTML = newStyleStr;
    }
  }
}

Like other software companies, we seek to responsibly disclose vulnerabilities in our products to our customers while also mitigating the risk that bad actors seek to exploit those vulnerabilities by releasing updates to our products that remediate these vulnerabilities before we disclose them.</p><p>For the latest update on our investigation, please read <a href="https://www.solarwinds.com/blog/new-findings-from-our-investigation-of-sunburst" dld="this blog embed" dlt="Media Overview">this blog</a>, and to learn more about the steps we’re taking to ensure the security and performance of the products we deliver, go <a href="https://www.solarwinds.com/blog/our-plan-for-a-safer-solarwinds-and-customer-community" dld="here embed" dlt="Media Overview">here</a>. You can also <a href="/shared-content/rss-feed/solarwinds-cve-rss-feed.xml" dld="Subscribe to this RSS Feed embed" dlt="Media Overview" target="_blank"><strong>Subscribe to this RSS Feed</strong></a> to be notified when we update this page (note: you will need to cut and paste the "Subscribe to this RSS feed" URL into an RSS Feed Reader, e.g. Outlook's RSS Subscriptions, to monitor updates).</p><p>A detailed Frequently Asked Questions (FAQ) page is available <a href="https://www.solarwinds.com/sa-overview/securityadvisory/faq" dld="here embed" dlt="Media Overview">here</a>, and we intend to update this page as we learn more information.</p></div></div></div> <button data-automation-id="expandable-text-button" variant="tertiary" class="text-button-tertiary-content hover:text-button-tertiary-content-hover active:text-button-tertiary-content-pressed disabled:text-button-tertiary-content-disabled hover:underline disabled:cursor-not-allowed text-link-m-mobile sm:text-link-m font-bold mt-4 hidden relative"><span class="flex flex-row items-center"><span class="">Read More</span><svg width="10" height="6" viewBox="0 0 10 6" fill="currentColor" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="inline ml-1.25 w-[14px]"><path d="M5 6 0 0h10L5 6z" fill="currentColor"></path></svg></span></button></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></section><style data-id="builderio-block" nonce="">    </style><section data-theme="white" data-automation-id="glossary-rail-entry" builder-id="builder-ec3d9e0541b4fba01c85192007bab0d4" class="builder-ec3d9e0541b4fba01c85192007bab0d4 builder-block"><style data-id="builderio-block" nonce="">.builder-5c52af2a85ad33c3dac2704531875b0f {

    font-size: var(--text-body-m, 1.125rem);

  }    </style><div builder-id="builder-79ed2b6095102579058ac4834b0260e7" class="builder-79ed2b6095102579058ac4834b0260e7 builder-block [&amp;_img]:my-4"><style data-id="builderio-block" nonce="">    </style><div builder-id="builder-261831a4f65fecb0ffa0919f1ab212c3" class="builder-261831a4f65fecb0ffa0919f1ab212c3 builder-block cs-rte-text"><div class="builder-text" style="outline:none"><p>As announced by SolarWinds President and CEO Sudhakar Ramakrishna in his Orange Matter blog, <a href="https://www.solarwinds.com/blog/our-plan-for-a-safer-solarwinds-and-customer-community" dld="Our Plan for a Safer SolarWinds and Customer Community embed" dlt="Glossary Rail Entry"><em>Our Plan for a Safer SolarWinds and Customer Community</em></a>, we’re taking key steps to ensure the security and integrity of the software we deliver to customers.</p></div></div><style data-id="builderio-block" nonce="">    </style><div builder-id="builder-6760a9591da509c6bddfa494ab829624" class="builder-6760a9591da509c6bddfa494ab829624 builder-block cs-rte-text"><div class="builder-text" style="outline:none"><p>SolarWinds uses a digital code-signing certificate to digitally sign each software build, and to help end users authenticate the code comes from us. As part of our response to the SUNBURST vulnerability, the code-signing certificate used by SolarWinds to sign the affected software versions was revoked <strong>March 8, 2021. This is industry-standard best practice for software that has been compromised.</strong></p></div></div><style data-id="builderio-block" nonce="">    </style><div builder-id="builder-538b9f2bf2e2399781e04f93768f1063" class="builder-538b9f2bf2e2399781e04f93768f1063 builder-block cs-rte-text"><div class="builder-text" style="outline:none"><p>We’ve obtained new digital code-signing certificates and have rebuilt the versions signed with the certificate to be revoked, have re-signed our code, and have re-released all of the products previously signed with the certificate to be revoked. To ensure the performance of your SolarWinds product(s), you must upgrade to these new builds.</p></div></div><style data-id="builderio-block" nonce="">    </style><div builder-id="builder-47706436dc1f4cc3342109deab440f28" class="builder-47706436dc1f4cc3342109deab440f28 builder-block cs-rte-text"><div class="builder-text" style="outline:none"><p>For full details on this part of our response to the SUNBURST vulnerability, please visit our <strong>SolarWinds New Digital Code-Signing Certificate</strong> page at <a href="https://www.solarwinds.com/sa-overview/new-digital-certificate" dld="solarwinds.com/sa-overview/new-digital-certificate  embed" dlt="Glossary Rail Entry">solarwinds.com/sa-overview/new-digital-certificate</a>.</p></div></div></div><style data-id="builderio-block" nonce="">.builder-bd21229df46036a39e8d7ae398e3c0ed {

}</style><div class="builder-blocks min-w-0 props-blocks-wrapper-b46bf284" builder-path="component.options.navItems.1.blocks" builder-parent-id="builder-22b392d8dda136e71783537a1477a223"><style data-id="builderio-block" nonce="">    </style><div id="about-supernova" builder-id="builder-79860b5b48766cf72d944751f958400a" class="builder-79860b5b48766cf72d944751f958400a builder-block"><style data-id="builderio-block" nonce="">.builder-ff6c15a159dbb8b2dfdf32fdb5657568 {

  }
    } </style><div builder-id="builder-ff6c15a159dbb8b2dfdf32fdb5657568" class="builder-ff6c15a159dbb8b2dfdf32fdb5657568 builder-block"><div class="builder-text" style="outline:none"><h3>ABOUT SUPERNOVA</h3></div></div><style data-id="builderio-block" nonce="">.builder-376d5938e0990e04e659e81b6e52208f {
    font-size: var(--text-body-m, 1.125rem);
line-height: var(--text-body-m--line-height, 2rem);
color: var(--color-body-primary, #444444);
  }    </style><div builder-id="builder-376d5938e0990e04e659e81b6e52208f" class="builder-376d5938e0990e04e659e81b6e52208f builder-block [&amp;_img]:my-4"><style data-id="builderio-block" nonce="">    </style><div builder-id="builder-c0d36cebff7b58a7bec84c19af1a5fd2" class="builder-c0d36cebff7b58a7bec84c19af1a5fd2 builder-block cs-rte-text"><div class="builder-text" style="outline:none"><p>SUPERNOVA is malware that was deployed using a vulnerability in the Orion Platform, and after the Orion Platform had been installed. Based on our investigation to date:</p></div></div><style data-id="builderio-block" nonce="">    </style><div builder-id="builder-e2f55e0922da90df9ed0dda8b589d13c" class="builder-e2f55e0922da90df9ed0dda8b589d13c builder-block cs-rte-text"><div class="builder-text" style="outline:none"><ul><li>SUPERNOVA is not malicious code embedded within the builds of our Orion<sup>®</sup> Platform as a supply chain attack. It is malware that is separately placed on a server that requires unauthorized access to a customer’s network and is designed to appear to be part of a SolarWinds product.</li><li>The SUPERNOVA malware consisted of two components. The first was a malicious, unsigned webshell .dll “app_web_logoimagehandler.ashx.b6031896.dll” specifically written to be used on the SolarWinds Orion Platform. The second is the utilization of a vulnerability in the Orion Platform to enable deployment of the malicious code. This vulnerability in the Orion Platform has been resolved in the latest updates.</li></ul></div></div><style data-id="builderio-block" nonce="">    </style><div builder-id="builder-f8b9c7f66d964f807d8bc60af0689810" class="builder-f8b9c7f66d964f807d8bc60af0689810 builder-block cs-rte-text"><div class="builder-text" style="outline:none"><p>We constantly work to enhance the security of our products and to protect our customers and ourselves because hackers and other cybercriminals are always seeking new ways to find and attack their victims. We work closely with our customers to address and remediate any potential concerns, and we encourage all customers to run only supported versions of our products and to upgrade to the latest versions to the get the full benefit of our updates, improvements, and enhancements.</p></div></div></div><style data-id="builderio-block" nonce="">.builder-9a204fa266936459f35cb420d49de9f5 {
    display: flex;
flex-direction: row;
align-items: center;
column-gap: var(--spacing-8, 32px);
margin-top: var(--spacing-8, 32px);
  }    </style><div builder-id="builder-9a204fa266936459f35cb420d49de9f5" class="builder-9a204fa266936459f35cb420d49de9f5 builder-block"></div></div></div><style>.props-blocks-wrapper-b46bf284 {
  display: flex;
  flex-direction: column;
  align-items: stretch;
}</style><div class="builder-blocks min-w-0 props-blocks-wrapper-b46bf284" builder-path="component.options.navItems.2.blocks" builder-parent-id="builder-22b392d8dda136e71783537a1477a223"><style data-id="builderio-block" nonce="">    </style><div id="about-sunburst" builder-id="builder-dddc440e5928c6bb035e03b594dea022" class="builder-dddc440e5928c6bb035e03b594dea022 builder-block"><style data-id="builderio-block" nonce="">.builder-6674990b1e79e6eea2f87b92016a24e2 {
    color: var(--color-headline, #111111);
font-weight: var(--font-weight-normal, 400);
font-size: var(--text-headline-m, 2.375rem);
line-height: var(--text-headline-m--line-height, 3rem);
margin-bottom: var(--spacing-4, 16px);
  }   @media (max-width: 639px) {
      .builder-6674990b1e79e6eea2f87b92016a24e2 {
    font-size: var(--text-subhead-xl, 1.875rem);
line-height: var(--text-subhead-l--line-height, 2.375rem);
  }
    } </style><div builder-id="builder-6674990b1e79e6eea2f87b92016a24e2" class="builder-6674990b1e79e6eea2f87b92016a24e2 builder-block"><div class="builder-text" style="outline:none"><h3>ABOUT SUNBURST</h3></div></div><style data-id="builderio-block" nonce="">.builder-c1507cb259f19eaf1074ad8ec856d7d1 {
    font-size: var(--text-body-m, 1.125rem);
line-height: var(--text-body-m--line-height, 2rem);
color: var(--color-body-primary, #444444);
  }    </style><div builder-id="builder-c1507cb259f19eaf1074ad8ec856d7d1" class="builder-c1507cb259f19eaf1074ad8ec856d7d1 builder-block [&amp;_img]:my-4"><style data-id="builderio-block" nonce="">    </style><div builder-id="builder-d64630927594208cccb6c8d39186b15a" class="builder-d64630927594208cccb6c8d39186b15a builder-block cs-rte-text"><div class="builder-text" style="outline:none"><p>SolarWinds and our customers were the victims of a cyberattack to our systems that inserted a vulnerability (SUNBURST) within our Orion<sup>®</sup> Platform software builds for versions <strong>2019.4 HF 5, 2020.2 </strong><u><strong>unpatched</strong></u><strong>,</strong> and <strong>2020.2 HF 1</strong>, which, if present and activated, could potentially allow an attacker to compromise the server on which the Orion products run. This attack was a very sophisticated supply chain attack, which refers to a disruption in a standard process resulting in a compromised result with a goal of being able to attack subsequent users of the software. In this case, it appears that the code was intended to be used in a targeted way as its exploitation requires manual intervention. We’ve been advised that the nature of this attack indicates that it may have been conducted by an outside nation state, but SolarWinds has not verified the identity of the attacker.</p></div></div><style data-id="builderio-block" nonce="">    </style><div builder-id="builder-f9914b13e49177a3f041b5067b5fe6a6" class="builder-f9914b13e49177a3f041b5067b5fe6a6 builder-block cs-rte-text"><div class="builder-text" style="outline:none"><p>As our investigation has progressed, and as we’ve worked with CrowdStrike and KPMG, we’ve identified malware known as SUNSPOT, the highly sophisticated and novel code designed to inject the SUNBURST malicious code into the Orion Platform during the build process. SUNSPOT is not a new malware or attack, but instead a component of the SUNBURST cyberattack. Read more about SUNSPOT on the CrowdStrike blog <a href="https://www.crowdstrike.com/blog/sunspot-malware-technical-analysis/" dld="here embed" dlt="Glossary Rail Entry">here</a>.</p></div></div><style data-id="builderio-block" nonce="">    </style><div builder-id="builder-98a6684c5a877a5a319aaf15477719a7" class="builder-98a6684c5a877a5a319aaf15477719a7 builder-block cs-rte-text"><div class="builder-text" style="outline:none"><p>While SUNSPOT is the means by which the attackers injected the SUNBURST backdoor during the build process of the Orion Platform, TEARDROP and RAINDROP are reportedly malware loaders that could be deployed as secondary tools using the SUNBURST backdoor. SUNSPOT, TEARDROP, and RAINDROP <strong>are NOT new vulnerabilities</strong> within our products as some reports in the media have indicated, but instead, they <strong>are elements of the SUNBURST attack chain</strong>.</p></div></div><style data-id="builderio-block" nonce="">    </style><div builder-id="builder-e93d99f41d103d55dec1e726a5eb128a" class="builder-e93d99f41d103d55dec1e726a5eb128a builder-block cs-rte-text"><div class="builder-text" style="outline:none"><p>The Cybersecurity and Infrastructure Security Agency (CISA) Computer Emergency Readiness Team (CERT), part of the Department of Homeland Security (DHS), CERT issued <a href="https://www.cisa.gov/news-events/directives/ed-21-01-mitigate-solarwinds-orion-code-compromise" dld="Emergency Directive 21-01 embed" dlt="Glossary Rail Entry">Emergency Directive 21-01</a> on December 13, 2020 regarding this issue and has updated their guidance as part of our ongoing coordination with the agency. The latest information can be found on CISA’s <a href="https://www.cisa.gov/news-events/alerts/2021/01/07/supply-chain-compromise" dld="Supply Chain Compromise embed" dlt="Glossary Rail Entry">Supply Chain Compromise</a> page and continues to be updated as we learn more.</p></div></div><style data-id="builderio-block" nonce="">    </style><div builder-id="builder-93adcf7c325aaac839a4d886a0326ea5" class="builder-93adcf7c325aaac839a4d886a0326ea5 builder-block cs-rte-text"><div class="builder-text" style="outline:none"><p><strong>We want to assure you we’ve removed the software builds known to be affected by the SUNBURST vulnerability from our download sites.</strong></p></div></div><style data-id="builderio-block" nonce="">    </style><div builder-id="builder-3e7fcd3c08c1d0354a59b603a01e7543" class="builder-3e7fcd3c08c1d0354a59b603a01e7543 builder-block cs-rte-text"><div class="builder-text" style="outline:none"><p>While our <a href="https://www.solarwinds.com/blog/new-findings-from-our-investigation-of-sunburst" dld="investigations are ongoing embed" dlt="Glossary Rail Entry">investigations are ongoing</a>, based on our investigations to date, we are not aware that this SUNBURST vulnerability affects other versions of Orion Platform products. Also, while we are still investigating our non-Orion products, we have not seen any evidence that they are impacted by the SUNBURST vulnerability.</p></div></div><style data-id="builderio-block" nonce="">    </style><div builder-id="builder-76724298796261686211d166db5e59e5" class="builder-76724298796261686211d166db5e59e5 builder-block cs-rte-text"><div class="builder-text" style="outline:none"><p>If you aren't sure which version of the Orion Platform you are using, see directions on how to check that <a href="https://support.solarwinds.com/SuccessCenter/s/article/Determine-which-version-of-a-SolarWinds-Orion-product-I-have-installed?language=en_US" dld="here embed" dlt="Glossary Rail Entry">here</a>. To check which hotfix updates you have applied, please go <a href="https://support.solarwinds.com/SuccessCenter/s/article/Verify-hotfixes-that-have-been-installed?language=en_US" dld="here embed" dlt="Glossary Rail Entry">here</a>.</p></div></div><style data-id="builderio-block" nonce="">    </style><div builder-id="builder-a8da220f2eb9c5719fe299e70cdcd35c" class="builder-a8da220f2eb9c5719fe299e70cdcd35c builder-block cs-rte-text"><div class="builder-text" style="outline:none"><p><strong>Known affected products:</strong> Orion Platform }</style><div class="builder-blocks min-w-0 props-blocks-wrapper-b46bf284" builder-path="component.options.navItems.3.blocks" builder-parent-id="builder-22b392d8dda136e71783537a1477a223"><style data-id="builderio-block" nonce="">    </style><div id="recommended-actions" builder-id="builder-629bf7a6f57361c74dda82234c41160e" class="builder-629bf7a6f57361c74dda82234c41160e builder-block"><style data-id="builderio-block" nonce="">.builder-c1da0edbc18e3a7fb420bf843a01472b {

    font-size: var(--text-subhead-xl, 1.875rem);

    } </style><div builder-id="builder-c1da0edbc18e3a7fb420bf843a01472b" class="builder-c1da0edbc18e3a7fb420bf843a01472b builder-block"><div class="builder-text" style="outline:none"><h3>RECOMMENDED ACTIONS</h3></div></div><style data-id="builderio-block" nonce="">.builder-b5ffe9ce35be58f04ebacc63437eb79c {
    font-size: var(--text-body-m, 1.125rem);
line-height: var(--text-body-m--line-height, 2rem);
color: var(--color-body-primary, #444444);
  }    </style><div builder-id="builder-b5ffe9ce35be58f04ebacc63437eb79c" class="builder-b5ffe9ce35be58f04ebacc63437eb79c builder-block [&amp;_img]:my-4"><style data-id="builderio-block" nonce="">    </style><div builder-id="builder-62414335080d835c8507fe95f84480f3" class="builder-62414335080d835c8507fe95f84480f3 builder-block cs-rte-text"><div class="builder-text" style="outline:none"><p>SolarWinds uses a digital code-signing certificate to digitally sign each software build, and to help end users authenticate the code comes from us. As part of our response to the SUNBURST vulnerability, the code-signing certificate used by SolarWinds to sign the affected software versions was revoked <strong>March 8, 2021. This is industry-standard best practice for software that has been compromised.</strong></p></div></div><style data-id="builderio-block" nonce="">    </style><div builder-id="builder-df044e79713a26b73f49089fc38c44ef" class="builder-df044e79713a26b73f49089fc38c44ef builder-block cs-rte-text"><div class="builder-text" style="outline:none"><p>We’ve obtained new digital code-signing certificates and have rebuilt the affected versions, have re-signed our code, and have re-released all of the products previously signed with the certificate to be revoked. To ensure the performance of your SolarWinds product(s), you must upgrade to these new builds.</p></div></div><style data-id="builderio-block" nonce="">    </style><div builder-id="builder-22dfac22e95a1f54e07df0a83c771149" class="builder-22dfac22e95a1f54e07df0a83c771149 builder-block cs-rte-text"><div class="builder-text" style="outline:none"><p>If you’re unable to upgrade at this time, we have provided a script that customers can install to temporarily protect their environment against the SUPERNOVA malware<strong>***</strong>. The script is available at <a href="https://downloads.solarwinds.com/solarwinds/Support/SupernovaMitigation.zip" dld="https://downloads.solarwinds.com/solarwinds/Support/SupernovaMitigation.zip  embed" dlt="Glossary Rail Entry">https://downloads.solarwinds.com/solarwinds/Support/SupernovaMitigation.zip</a>.</p></div></div><style data-id="builderio-block" nonce="">    </style><div builder-id="builder-d46659157c111403a5f746ce0ba41702" class="builder-d46659157c111403a5f746ce0ba41702 builder-block cs-rte-text"><div class="builder-text" style="outline:none"><p>To take advantage of our latest available security updates protections for the products you have deployed, we recommend all active maintenance customers of Orion Platform products <strong>upgrade to version 2020.2.5</strong> as soon as possible. For more information, review the Release Notes <a href="https://documentation.solarwinds.com/en/success_center/orionplatform/content/release_notes/release_history.htm" dld="here  embed" dlt="Glossary Rail Entry">here</a>, and KB article <a href="https://support.solarwinds.com/SuccessCenter/s/article/Remote-Code-Execution-CVE-Frequently-Asked-Questions?language=en_US" dld="here embed" dlt="Glossary Rail Entry">here</a>.</p></div></div><style data-id="builderio-block" nonce="">    </style><div builder-id="builder-cf73c464b97c16e9e94ea3030607cc1f" class="builder-cf73c464b97c16e9e94ea3030607cc1f builder-block cs-rte-text"><div class="builder-text" style="outline:none"><p>Customers on <strong>Orion Platform versions 2019.4.2 or 2020.2.4</strong> have applied security enhancements designed to protect you from SUNBURST and SUPERNOVA. <strong>NOTE: </strong>If you reinstall, you need to re-apply the patch or hotfix.</p></div></div><style data-id="builderio-block" nonce="">    </style><div builder-id="builder-e29a6b1743e34ebb3f6982eb153a71d6" class="builder-e29a6b1743e34ebb3f6982eb153a71d6 builder-block cs-rte-text"><div class="builder-text" style="outline:none"><p>The latest updates designed to protect against SUNBURST and SUPERNOVA are as follows:</p></div></div><style data-id="builderio-block" nonce="">    </style><div builder-id="builder-d9424242747ed667bb71b5e5df11e985" February 2, 2021)</li><li>2020.2.4 (released January 25, 2021)</li><li>2019.2 Security Patch (released December 23, 2020)</li><li>2018.4 Security Patch (released December 23, 2020)</li><li>2018.2 Security Patch (released December 23, 2020)</li></ul></div></div><style data-id="builderio-block" nonce="">    </style><div builder-id="builder-dd7bbd4c2efaf80b3bc033e61eea29a9"
